          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

TALOS-2021-1398



<span class="line"><!---->TALOS-2021-1398<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Google Chrome MediaStreamTrackGenerator use after free vulnerability



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome MediaStreamTrackGenerator use after free vulnerability<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Summary



<span class="line"><!---->Summary<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A potential code execution vulnerability exists in the MediaStreamTrackGenerator functionality of Google Chrome 94.0.4606.81 (Stable) and 97.0.4674.1 (Canary). A specially-crafted web page can lead to use after free. An attacker can provide a malicious web site to trigger this vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->A potential code execution vulnerability exists in the MediaStreamTrackGenerator functionality of Google Chrome 94.0.4606.81 (Stable) and 97.0.4674.1 (Canary). A specially-crafted web page can lead to use after free. An attacker can provide a malicious web site to trigger this vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Tested Versions



<span class="line"><!---->Tested Versions<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Google Chrome 94.0.4606.81 (Stable) 



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome 94.0.4606.81 (Stable) <!----></span>



<br>





Google Chrome 97.0.4674.1 (Canary)



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome 97.0.4674.1 (Canary)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Product URLs



<span class="line"><!---->Product URLs<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://www.google.com/chrome/



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://www.google.com/chrome/"><!---->https://www.google.com/chrome/<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





CVSSv3 Score



<span class="line"><!---->CVSSv3 Score<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





8.3 - CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:L



<span class="line"><!---->8.3 - CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:R/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:L<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CWE



<span class="line"><!---->CWE<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





CWE-416 - Use After Free



<span class="line"><!---->CWE-416 - Use After Free<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Details



<span class="line"><!---->Details<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Google Chrome is a cross-platform web browser, developed by Google.



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome is a cross-platform web browser, developed by Google.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The vulnerability exists in object MediaStreamTrackGenerator which is responsible for creating streams of audio/video.



<span class="line"><!---->The vulnerability exists in object MediaStreamTrackGenerator which is responsible for creating streams of audio/video.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





MediaStreamTrackGenerator inherits from MediaStreamTrack. Thanks to this inheritance the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object can be cloned/copied to new object, see function below .



<span class="line"><!---->MediaStreamTrackGenerator inherits from MediaStreamTrack. Thanks to this inheritance the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object can be cloned/copied to new object, see function below .<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





 1:      MediaStreamTrack* MediaStreamTrack::cloneMediaStreamTrack::clone(ScriptState* script_state) {



<span class="line"><!----> 1:      MediaStreamTrack* MediaStreamTrack::cloneMediaStreamTrack::clone(ScriptState* script_state) {<!----></span>



<br>





 2:      SendLogMessage(String::Format("%s()", __func__));



<span class="line"><!----> 2:      SendLogMessage(String::Format("%s()", __func__));<!----></span>



<br>





 3:      MediaStreamComponent* cloned_component = Component()->Clone();



<span class="line"><!----> 3:      MediaStreamComponent* cloned_component = Component()-&gt;Clone();<!----></span>



<br>





 4:      MediaStreamTrack* cloned_track = MakeGarbageCollected<MediaStreamTrack>(



<span class="line"><!----> 4:      MediaStreamTrack* cloned_track = MakeGarbageCollected&lt;MediaStreamTrack&gt;(<!----></span>



<br>





 5:          ExecutionContext::From(script_state), cloned_component, ready_state_,



<span class="line"><!----> 5:          ExecutionContext::From(script_state), cloned_component, ready_state_,<!----></span>



<br>





 6:          base::DoNothing());



<span class="line"><!----> 6:          base::DoNothing());<!----></span>



<br>





 7:      DidCloneMediaStreamTrack(Component(), cloned_component);



<span class="line"><!----> 7:      DidCloneMediaStreamTrack(Component(), cloned_component);<!----></span>



<br>





 8:      if (image_capture_) {



<span class="line"><!----> 8:      if (image_capture_) {<!----></span>



<br>





 9:          cloned_track->image_capture_ = image_capture_->Clone();



<span class="line"><!----> 9:          cloned_track-&gt;image_capture_ = image_capture_-&gt;Clone();<!----></span>



<br>





10:      }



<span class="line"><!---->10:      }<!----></span>



<br>





11:      return cloned_track;



<span class="line"><!---->11:      return cloned_track;<!----></span>



<br>





12:      }



<span class="line"><!---->12:      }<!----></span>



<br>





The above function is resposible for making the copy of the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object, the allocation of new memory happens at line 4. By definition when using MakeGarbageCollected, the new object wont be deleted by delete but using Olipan, which is the Chromium garbage collector.



<span class="line"><!---->The above function is resposible for making the copy of the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object, the allocation of new memory happens at line 4. By definition when using MakeGarbageCollected, the new object wont be deleted by delete but using Olipan, which is the Chromium garbage collector.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





You can create an instance of your class through MakeGarbageCollected<T>, while you may not free the object with delete, 



<span class="line"><!---->You can create an instance of your class through MakeGarbageCollected&lt;T&gt;, while you may not free the object with delete, <!----></span>



<br>





as Oilpan is responsible for deallocating the object once it determines the object is unreachable.



<span class="line"><!---->as Oilpan is responsible for deallocating the object once it determines the object is unreachable.<!----></span>



<br>





During streaming we can abort the stream using the JS function abort, which corresponds to the C++ code shown below.



<span class="line"><!---->During streaming we can abort the stream using the JS function abort, which corresponds to the C++ code shown below.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1:      ScriptPromise MediaStreamAudioTrackUnderlyingSink::abort(



<span class="line"><!---->1:      ScriptPromise MediaStreamAudioTrackUnderlyingSink::abort(<!----></span>



<br>





2:          ScriptState* script_state,



<span class="line"><!---->2:          ScriptState* script_state,<!----></span>



<br>





3:          ScriptValue reason,



<span class="line"><!---->3:          ScriptValue reason,<!----></span>



<br>





4:          ExceptionState& exception_state) {



<span class="line"><!---->4:          ExceptionState&amp; exception_state) {<!----></span>



<br>





5:      DCHECK_CALLED_ON_VALID_SEQUENCE(sequence_checker_);



<span class="line"><!---->5:      DCHECK_CALLED_ON_VALID_SEQUENCE(sequence_checker_);<!----></span>



<br>





6:      Disconnect();



<span class="line"><!---->6:      Disconnect();<!----></span>



<br>





7:      return ScriptPromise::CastUndefined(script_state);



<span class="line"><!---->7:      return ScriptPromise::CastUndefined(script_state);<!----></span>



<br>





8:      }



<span class="line"><!---->8:      }<!----></span>



<br>





The interesting part happens at line 6, where the stream gets disconnected which triggers destructor of the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object. 



<span class="line"><!---->The interesting part happens at line 6, where the stream gets disconnected which triggers destructor of the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object. <!----></span>



<br>





However we still have copy of this object which was marked by Olipan. This process can be interrupted using Events, one of those events is onended which is triggered when status of the stream is changed. 



<span class="line"><!---->However we still have copy of this object which was marked by Olipan. This process can be interrupted using Events, one of those events is onended which is triggered when status of the stream is changed. <!----></span>



<br>





During this event we can try to free once again the cloned MediaStreamTrackGenerator which would lead to use-after-free vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->During this event we can try to free once again the cloned MediaStreamTrackGenerator which would lead to use-after-free vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





With proper manipulation of objects, when onended event is executed, this vulnerability could lead to control over freed memory and ultimately arbitrary code execution.



<span class="line"><!---->With proper manipulation of objects, when onended event is executed, this vulnerability could lead to control over freed memory and ultimately arbitrary code execution.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

I was not able to reproduce, for whatever reason - it looks like it requires the right timing and the POC here might not hit it for me. Regardless...



<span class="line"><!---->I was not able to reproduce, for whatever reason - it looks like it requires the right timing and the POC here might not hit it for me. Regardless...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





MediaStreamTrack::MediaStreamTrack(ExecutionContext* context,



<span class="line"><!---->MediaStreamTrack::MediaStreamTrack(ExecutionContext* context,<!----></span>



<br>





                                   MediaStreamComponent* component,



<span class="line"><!---->                                   MediaStreamComponent* component,<!----></span>



<br>





                                   MediaStreamSource::ReadyState ready_state,



<span class="line"><!---->                                   MediaStreamSource::ReadyState ready_state,<!----></span>



<br>





                                   base::OnceClosure callback)



<span class="line"><!---->                                   base::OnceClosure callback)<!----></span>



<br>





    : ready_state_(ready_state),



<span class="line"><!---->    : ready_state_(ready_state),<!----></span>



<br>





      component_(component),



<span class="line"><!---->      component_(component),<!----></span>



<br>





      execution_context_(context) {



<span class="line"><!---->      execution_context_(context) {<!----></span>



<br>





  component_->Source()->AddObserver(this);



<span class="line"><!---->  component_-&gt;Source()-&gt;AddObserver(this);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





My observations:



<span class="line"><!---->My observations:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. MediaStreamTrack observes MediaStreamSource, which holds a WeakMember<Observer> pointer to MediaStreamTrack.



<span class="line"><!---->1. MediaStreamTrack observes MediaStreamSource, which holds a WeakMember&lt;Observer&gt; pointer to MediaStreamTrack.<!----></span>



<br>





2. MediaStreamTrack does not remove itself as an observer.



<span class="line"><!---->2. MediaStreamTrack does not remove itself as an observer.<!----></span>



<br>





3. MediaStreamSource::SetReadyState() walks those weak pointers and and calls SourceChangedState.



<span class="line"><!---->3. MediaStreamSource::SetReadyState() walks those weak pointers and and calls SourceChangedState.<!----></span>



<br>





4. The POC makes 2 MediaStreamTracks (via clone()). This means MediaStreamSource has 2 weak pointers as observers.



<span class="line"><!---->4. The POC makes 2 MediaStreamTracks (via clone()). This means MediaStreamSource has 2 weak pointers as observers.<!----></span>



<br>





5.  The POC also makes a MediaStreamAudioTrackUnderlyingSink via MediaStreamTrackGenerator::writable().



<span class="line"><!---->5.  The POC also makes a MediaStreamAudioTrackUnderlyingSink via MediaStreamTrackGenerator::writable().<!----></span>



<br>





6. Step 5 gives access to an abort() that will use both MediaStreamTracks by weak pointer, through Step 1.



<span class="line"><!---->6. Step 5 gives access to an abort() that will use both MediaStreamTracks by weak pointer, through Step 1.<!----></span>



<br>





8. The JS is holding a reference to both MediaStreamTracks



<span class="line"><!---->8. The JS is holding a reference to both MediaStreamTracks<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





What I am missing is a step 9 where abort() actually frees the MediaStreamSource.



<span class="line"><!---->What I am missing is a step 9 where abort() actually frees the MediaStreamSource.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





> The interesting part happens at line 6, where the stream gets disconnected which triggers destructor of the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object. 



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; The interesting part happens at line 6, where the stream gets disconnected which triggers destructor of the MediaStreamTrackGenerator object. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Did you not get a "freed" stack trace from ASAN as well? Can you provide it? I can't locate how it would be freed.



<span class="line"><!---->Did you not get a "freed" stack trace from ASAN as well? Can you provide it? I can't locate how it would be freed.<!----></span>

From what we can tell gc() forces the garbage collector to run so it is run twice on the same object.



<span class="line"><!---->From what we can tell gc() forces the garbage collector to run so it is run twice on the same object.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Because it's not a regular malloc/free that's happening, ASAN isn't detecting it as a UAF, but it's detecting that freed memory is being used that's why it doesn't provide the location that memory is being freed.



<span class="line"><!---->Because it's not a regular malloc/free that's happening, ASAN isn't detecting it as a UAF, but it's detecting that freed memory is being used that's why it doesn't provide the location that memory is being freed.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





See 



<span class="line"><!---->See <!----></span>





https://github.com/google/sanitizers/issues/191



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://github.com/google/sanitizers/issues/191"><!---->https://github.com/google/sanitizers/issues/191<!----></a>





 for more info



<span class="line"><!----> for more info<!----></span>

Oilpan as a Mark/Sweep GC that first marks a heap and then reclaims objects. Between marking and sweeping, objects are poisoned. WeakMember are synchronously cleared after marking.



<span class="line"><!---->Oilpan as a Mark/Sweep GC that first marks a heap and then reclaims objects. Between marking and sweeping, objects are poisoned. WeakMember are synchronously cleared after marking.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I have not run the repro yet.



<span class="line"><!---->I have not run the repro yet.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





IIUC then MediaStreamSource is actually poisoned. Since WebPlatformMediaStreamSource::owner_ is a weak ptr it should have been cleared already at this point.



<span class="line"><!---->IIUC then MediaStreamSource is actually poisoned. Since WebPlatformMediaStreamSource::owner_ is a weak ptr it should have been cleared already at this point.<!----></span>

Sorry, I didn't see the observer parts. The issue is here:



<span class="line"><!---->Sorry, I didn't see the observer parts. The issue is here:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





void MediaStreamSource::SetReadyState(ReadyState ready_state) {



<span class="line"><!---->void MediaStreamSource::SetReadyState(ReadyState ready_state) {<!----></span>



<br>





  SendLogMessage(String::Format("SetReadyState({id=%s}, {ready_state=%s})",



<span class="line"><!---->  SendLogMessage(String::Format("SetReadyState({id=%s}, {ready_state=%s})",<!----></span>



<br>





                                Id().Utf8().c_str(),



<span class="line"><!---->                                Id().Utf8().c_str(),<!----></span>



<br>





                                ReadyStateToString(ready_state))



<span class="line"><!---->                                ReadyStateToString(ready_state))<!----></span>



<br>





                     .Utf8());



<span class="line"><!---->                     .Utf8());<!----></span>



<br>





  if (ready_state_ != kReadyStateEnded && ready_state_ != ready_state) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (ready_state_ != kReadyStateEnded &amp;&amp; ready_state_ != ready_state) {<!----></span>



<br>





    ready_state_ = ready_state;



<span class="line"><!---->    ready_state_ = ready_state;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    // Observers may dispatch events which create and add new Observers;



<span class="line"><!---->    // Observers may dispatch events which create and add new Observers;<!----></span>



<br>





    // take a snapshot so as to safely iterate.



<span class="line"><!---->    // take a snapshot so as to safely iterate.<!----></span>



<br>





    Vector<base::OnceClosure> observer_callbacks;



<span class="line"><!---->    Vector&lt;base::OnceClosure&gt; observer_callbacks;<!----></span>



<br>





    for (auto it = observers_.begin(); it != observers_.end(); ++it) {



<span class="line"><!---->    for (auto it = observers_.begin(); it != observers_.end(); ++it) {<!----></span>



<br>





      observer_callbacks.push_back(



<span class="line"><!---->      observer_callbacks.push_back(<!----></span>



<br>





          base::BindOnce(&Observer::SourceChangedState, *it)); <====== This is not binding the oberver strongly.



<span class="line"><!---->          base::BindOnce(&amp;Observer::SourceChangedState, *it)); &lt;====== This is not binding the oberver strongly.<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





    for (auto& observer_callback : observer_callbacks) {



<span class="line"><!---->    for (auto&amp; observer_callback : observer_callbacks) {<!----></span>



<br>





      std::move(observer_callback).Run(); <===== callbacks themselves may allocate and invoke GC which may reclaim the weak observers.



<span class="line"><!---->      std::move(observer_callback).Run(); &lt;===== callbacks themselves may allocate and invoke GC which may reclaim the weak observers.<!----></span>



<br>





    }



<span class="line"><!---->    }<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





tl;dr: The receiver was not properly bound strongly until the callbacks were executed. This is a problem if callbacks themselves are generic and thus allocate and invoke GC.



<span class="line"><!---->tl;dr: The receiver was not properly bound strongly until the callbacks were executed. This is a problem if callbacks themselves are generic and thus allocate and invoke GC.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Quickfix is here: 



<span class="line"><!---->Quickfix is here: <!----></span>





https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3247159



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3247159"><!---->https://chromium-review.googlesource.com/c/chromium/src/+/3247159<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





I thought that Blink mandates the use of WTF::Bind() to be used instead of base::BindOnce.



<span class="line"><!---->I thought that Blink mandates the use of WTF::Bind() to be used instead of base::BindOnce.<!----></span>

> For my learning: Why does the callback need a Persistent<T> and not a WeakPersistent<T>?



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; For my learning: Why does the callback need a Persistent&lt;T&gt; and not a WeakPersistent&lt;T&gt;?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Persistent will make sure the callback gets fired.



<span class="line"><!---->Persistent will make sure the callback gets fired.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





WeakPersistent should in theory allow that the callback gets cancelled if the observer gets executed until then. I think this is controlled somewhere through Unwrap traits. (I fail to find the codesearch place now).



<span class="line"><!---->WeakPersistent should in theory allow that the callback gets cancelled if the observer gets executed until then. I think this is controlled somewhere through Unwrap traits. (I fail to find the codesearch place now).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Not sure what the intended semantics here is, maybe media folks can clarify.



<span class="line"><!---->Not sure what the intended semantics here is, maybe media folks can clarify.<!----></span>

Ah, so iterating a set of WeakMember<T> gives you T* entries, not WeakMember<T>, or WeakPersistent<T>..?



<span class="line"><!---->Ah, so iterating a set of WeakMember&lt;T&gt; gives you T* entries, not WeakMember&lt;T&gt;, or WeakPersistent&lt;T&gt;..?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I don't see that in the traits. I think a WeakMember<T> should give a const WeakMember<T>&: 



<span class="line"><!---->I don't see that in the traits. I think a WeakMember&lt;T&gt; should give a const WeakMember&lt;T&gt;&amp;: <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/platform/wtf/hash_traits.h;drc=5539ecff898c79b0771340051d62bf81649e448d;l=134



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/platform/wtf/hash_traits.h;drc=5539ecff898c79b0771340051d62bf81649e448d;l=134"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/platform/wtf/hash_traits.h;drc=5539ecff898c79b0771340051d62bf81649e448d;l=134<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





But WeakMember<T> also converts to T* implicitly: 



<span class="line"><!---->But WeakMember&lt;T&gt; also converts to T* implicitly: <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/include/cppgc/member.h;drc=5539ecff898c79b0771340051d62bf81649e448d;l=179



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/include/cppgc/member.h;drc=5539ecff898c79b0771340051d62bf81649e448d;l=179"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/include/cppgc/member.h;drc=5539ecff898c79b0771340051d62bf81649e448d;l=179<!----></a>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
